====================================================================================================

<span class="text-4505230f--UIH300-2063425d--textUIFamily-5ebd8e40--text-8ee2c8b2"></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--UIH300-2063425d--textUIFamily-5ebd8e40--text-8ee2c8b2"></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--UIH300-2063425d--textUIFamily-5ebd8e40--text-8ee2c8b2"></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1292161879984fd1861860335dd0a56b"><span data-offset-key="1292161879984fd1861860335dd0a56b:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="42064f7228e64f2c9dead283f3ab31e1"><span data-offset-key="42064f7228e64f2c9dead283f3ab31e1:0">**Requests**</span><span data-offset-key="42064f7228e64f2c9dead283f3ab31e1:1"> is an elegant and simple HTTP library for Python, built for human beings.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="223f7e8ffae3441ab4cc5811a93ea26e"><span data-offset-key="223f7e8ffae3441ab4cc5811a93ea26e:0">**Behold, the power of Requests**</span><span data-offset-key="223f7e8ffae3441ab4cc5811a93ea26e:1">:</span></span></span>

    >>> r = requests.get('https://api.github.com/user', auth=('user', 'pass'))>>> r.status_code200>>> r.headers['content-type']'application/json; charset=utf8'>>> r.encoding'utf-8'>>> r.text'{"type":"User"...'>>> r.json(){'private_gists': 419, 'total_private_repos': 77, ...}

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c042c31050404a9ea5faacc31911a711"><span data-offset-key="c042c31050404a9ea5faacc31911a711:0">See </span></span><a href="https://gist.github.com/973705" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f6ecd1b7722b475c8171d9fef958167f"><span data-offset-key="f6ecd1b7722b475c8171d9fef958167f:0">similar code, sans Requests</span></span></a><span data-key="e3cf849ecec44e6dba6b308ef8b403c0"><span data-offset-key="e3cf849ecec44e6dba6b308ef8b403c0:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e256c0af309546f9af279b72d25be807"><span data-offset-key="e256c0af309546f9af279b72d25be807:0">**Requests**</span><span data-offset-key="e256c0af309546f9af279b72d25be807:1"> allows you to send HTTP/1.1 requests extremely easily. There’s no need to manually add query strings to your URLs, or to form-encode your POST data. Keep-alive and HTTP connection pooling are 100% automatic, thanks to </span></span><a href="https://github.com/urllib3/urllib3" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="bdb141ca484b4572976f11b42cfc64cf"><span data-offset-key="bdb141ca484b4572976f11b42cfc64cf:0">urllib3</span></span></a><span data-key="60dfaeef61964a1b9f4dddea20c96d9f"><span data-offset-key="60dfaeef61964a1b9f4dddea20c96d9f:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH600-23f228db--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="eaf2fb9f846c45b5a7504dcff402ff81"><span data-offset-key="eaf2fb9f846c45b5a7504dcff402ff81:0">Beloved Features</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="796869762515425cb829baa77759549c"><span data-offset-key="796869762515425cb829baa77759549c:0">Requests is ready for today’s web.</span></span></span>

-   <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="62e45c792f67451c818fd8abb0276b0b"><span data-offset-key="62e45c792f67451c818fd8abb0276b0b:0">Keep-Alive & Connection Pooling</span></span></span>

Defaults to </span><span data-offset-key="f22c3a8581ad4721ade18ea2dd463994:2"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">True</code></span><span data-offset-key="f22c3a8581ad4721ade18ea2dd463994:3">.</span></span></span></p></div></li><li><div class="reset-3c756112--listItemContent-756c9114" data-key="571ea6b4ab6c447e9550bcaea7bc24cd"><p><span class="text-4505230f--UIH400-4e41e82a--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="f158a2ad87da4ad6894e588316570b2b"><span data-offset-key="f158a2ad87da4ad6894e588316570b2b:0"><strong>stream</strong></span><span data-offset-key="f158a2ad87da4ad6894e588316570b2b:1"> – (optional) if </span><span data-offset-key="f158a2ad87da4ad6894e588316570b2b:2"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">False</code></span><span data-offset-key="f158a2ad87da4ad6894e588316570b2b:3">, the response content will be immediately downloaded.</span></span></span></p></div></li><li><div class="reset-3c756112--listItemContent-756c9114" data-key="5a48f2a9e5b046fa8394df9f90263310"><p><span class="text-4505230f--UIH400-4e41e82a--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7d5eaf6b4cd940bd8e88de298efac01b"><span data-offset-key="7d5eaf6b4cd940bd8e88de298efac01b:0"><strong>cert</strong></span><span data-offset-key="7d5eaf6b4cd940bd8e88de298efac01b:1"> – (optional) if String, path to ssl client cert file (.pem). <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="622d04bca7ca487aa308496dc5eaf6d3"><span data-offset-key="622d04bca7ca487aa308496dc5eaf6d3:0">The server did not send any data in the allotted amount of time.</span><span data-offset-key="622d04bca7ca487aa308496dc5eaf6d3:1">*exception* </span><span data-offset-key="622d04bca7ca487aa308496dc5eaf6d3:2">`requests.Timeout`</span><span data-offset-key="622d04bca7ca487aa308496dc5eaf6d3:3">(</span><span data-offset-key="622d04bca7ca487aa308496dc5eaf6d3:4">*\*args*</span><span data-offset-key="622d04bca7ca487aa308496dc5eaf6d3:5">, </span><span data-offset-key="622d04bca7ca487aa308496dc5eaf6d3:6">*\*\*kwargs*</span><span data-offset-key="622d04bca7ca487aa308496dc5eaf6d3:7">)</span></span><a href="https://docs.python-requests.org/en/master/_modules/requests/exceptions/#Timeout" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="2736037105b04448a6aadca6ed0278f8"><span data-offset-key="2736037105b04448a6aadca6ed0278f8:0">[source]</span></span></a><span data-key="eb7ea7730098467faa3fe565db0382de"><span data-offset-key="eb7ea7730098467faa3fe565db0382de:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="4b005489b2194e46bbb807ab45eb2ad5"><span data-offset-key="4b005489b2194e46bbb807ab45eb2ad5:0">The request timed out.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b6caccb1fd2647178aa4cf72a895c5f3"><span data-offset-key="b6caccb1fd2647178aa4cf72a895c5f3:0">Catching this error will catch both </span><span data-offset-key="b6caccb1fd2647178aa4cf72a895c5f3:1">`ConnectTimeout`</span><span data-offset-key="b6caccb1fd2647178aa4cf72a895c5f3:2"> and </span><span data-offset-key="b6caccb1fd2647178aa4cf72a895c5f3:3">`ReadTimeout`</span><span data-offset-key="b6caccb1fd2647178aa4cf72a895c5f3:4"> errors.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7a8701c8bceb488dbf869267ad2e1985"><span data-offset-key="7a8701c8bceb488dbf869267ad2e1985:0">Constructs a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python-requests.org/en/master/api/#requests.PreparedRequest" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="9636143e5b534436bdddf59f7bf3b55e"><span data-offset-key="9636143e5b534436bdddf59f7bf3b55e:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">PreparedRequest</code></span></span></a><span data-key="49bf60264cd94ce59f0af91c4cf2ddfe"><span data-offset-key="49bf60264cd94ce59f0af91c4cf2ddfe:0"> for transmission and returns it. <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e1f3f0d7b0c4421bb4be8613ebf711d0"><span data-offset-key="e1f3f0d7b0c4421bb4be8613ebf711d0:0">`should_strip_auth`</span><span data-offset-key="e1f3f0d7b0c4421bb4be8613ebf711d0:1">(</span><span data-offset-key="e1f3f0d7b0c4421bb4be8613ebf711d0:2">*old\_url*</span><span data-offset-key="e1f3f0d7b0c4421bb4be8613ebf711d0:3">, </span><span data-offset-key="e1f3f0d7b0c4421bb4be8613ebf711d0:4">*new\_url*</span><span data-offset-key="e1f3f0d7b0c4421bb4be8613ebf711d0:5">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="8af067003bd54493b8b7e7cb50a6b11b"><span data-offset-key="8af067003bd54493b8b7e7cb50a6b11b:0">Decide whether Authorization header should be removed when redirecting</span><span data-offset-key="8af067003bd54493b8b7e7cb50a6b11b:1">`stream`</span><span data-offset-key="8af067003bd54493b8b7e7cb50a6b11b:2"> *= None*</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="22b3ddc3ad374145be10101cc7113269"><span data-offset-key="22b3ddc3ad374145be10101cc7113269:0">Stream response content default.</span><span data-offset-key="22b3ddc3ad374145be10101cc7113269:1">`trust_env`</span><span data-offset-key="22b3ddc3ad374145be10101cc7113269:2"> *= None*</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b99df42255104d5ebc889454b9a9f5a2"><span data-offset-key="b99df42255104d5ebc889454b9a9f5a2:0">Trust environment settings for proxy configuration, default authentication and similar.</span><span data-offset-key="b99df42255104d5ebc889454b9a9f5a2:1">`verify`</span><span data-offset-key="b99df42255104d5ebc889454b9a9f5a2:2"> *= None*</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d9efab2c9ac24ead94368d5e0266ec55"><span data-offset-key="d9efab2c9ac24ead94368d5e0266ec55:0">SSL Verification default. Defaults to True, requiring requests to verify the TLS certificate at the remote end. If verify is set to False, requests will accept any TLS certificate presented by the server, and will ignore hostname mismatches and/or expired certificates, which will make your application vulnerable to man-in-the-middle (MitM) attacks. Only set this to False for testing.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH600-23f228db--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6e2a41dbe8654df3b93d37fee51eda96"><span data-offset-key="6e2a41dbe8654df3b93d37fee51eda96:0">Lower-Level Classes</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="8dca1530aed74676af6b31c43652bf49"><span data-offset-key="8dca1530aed74676af6b31c43652bf49:0">This function eventually generates a </span><span data-offset-key="8dca1530aed74676af6b31c43652bf49:1">`Cookie`</span><span data-offset-key="8dca1530aed74676af6b31c43652bf49:2"> header from the given cookies using cookielib. <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="43532e5a8a4849639f770fecb3aa10a2"><span data-offset-key="43532e5a8a4849639f770fecb3aa10a2:0">Provides a general-case interface for Requests sessions to contact HTTP and HTTPS urls by implementing the Transport Adapter interface. This class will usually be created by the </span><span data-offset-key="43532e5a8a4849639f770fecb3aa10a2:1">`Session`</span><span data-offset-key="43532e5a8a4849639f770fecb3aa10a2:2"> class under the covers.</span></span></span>

Note, this applies only to failed DNS lookups, socket connections and connection timeouts, never to requests where data has made it to the server. By default, Requests does not retry failed connections. If you need granular control over the conditions under which we retry a request, import urllib3’s </span><span data-offset-key="ccc6ebc7ce384bc18a575adb7068f917:2"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">Retry</code></span><span data-offset-key="ccc6ebc7ce384bc18a575adb7068f917:3"> class and pass that instead.</span></span></span></p></div></li><li><div class="reset-3c756112--listItemContent-756c9114" data-key="8fc63f599f3241b2909e73b8b5951acd"><p><span class="text-4505230f--UIH400-4e41e82a--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5f56e24068e742999f71fa18e8f3d695"><span data-offset-key="5f56e24068e742999f71fa18e8f3d695:0"><strong>pool_block</strong></span><span data-offset-key="5f56e24068e742999f71fa18e8f3d695:1"> – Whether the connection pool should block for connections.</span></span></span></p></div></li></ul></td></tr></tbody></table>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5b4b5136539e4629bf082052e3087081"><span data-offset-key="5b4b5136539e4629bf082052e3087081:0">Add any headers needed by the connection. <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b14e6463ef6444d89050d81fa69ed0f1"><span data-offset-key="b14e6463ef6444d89050d81fa69ed0f1:0">Compatibility class; is a cookielib.CookieJar, but exposes a dict interface.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1b550c26c40a4508a0391393665780a7"><span data-offset-key="1b550c26c40a4508a0391393665780a7:0">This is the CookieJar we create by default for requests and sessions that don’t specify one, since some clients may expect response.cookies and session.cookies to support dict operations.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d33d52ccc2dc43fca6e9c44fb8c963f4"><span data-offset-key="d33d52ccc2dc43fca6e9c44fb8c963f4:0">Requests does not use the dict interface internally; it’s just for compatibility with external client code. All requests code should work out of the box with externally provided instances of </span><span data-offset-key="d33d52ccc2dc43fca6e9c44fb8c963f4:1">`CookieJar`</span><span data-offset-key="d33d52ccc2dc43fca6e9c44fb8c963f4:2">, e.g. </span><span data-offset-key="d33d52ccc2dc43fca6e9c44fb8c963f4:3">`LWPCookieJar`</span><span data-offset-key="d33d52ccc2dc43fca6e9c44fb8c963f4:4"> and </span><span data-offset-key="d33d52ccc2dc43fca6e9c44fb8c963f4:5">`FileCookieJar`</span><span data-offset-key="d33d52ccc2dc43fca6e9c44fb8c963f4:6">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="37b54a71a1de42cf8e3ab0970a3b8e49"><span data-offset-key="37b54a71a1de42cf8e3ab0970a3b8e49:0">Unlike a regular CookieJar, this class is pickleable.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="dc53719e01344b4c815ca382837f173f"><span data-offset-key="dc53719e01344b4c815ca382837f173f:0">Warning</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c3dc3be945ed4ff69e76c80de136e7e0"><span data-offset-key="c3dc3be945ed4ff69e76c80de136e7e0:0">dictionary operations that are normally O(1) may be O(n).</span><span data-offset-key="c3dc3be945ed4ff69e76c80de136e7e0:1">`add_cookie_header`</span><span data-offset-key="c3dc3be945ed4ff69e76c80de136e7e0:2">(</span><span data-offset-key="c3dc3be945ed4ff69e76c80de136e7e0:3">*request*</span><span data-offset-key="c3dc3be945ed4ff69e76c80de136e7e0:4">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5cf57d0c8f914a01aad942ea45f9814c"><span data-offset-key="5cf57d0c8f914a01aad942ea45f9814c:0">Add correct Cookie: header to request (urllib2.Request object).</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="21b064b731804b38acae1ad7d017785e"><span data-offset-key="21b064b731804b38acae1ad7d017785e:0">The Cookie2 header is also added unless policy.hide\_cookie2 is true.</span><span data-offset-key="21b064b731804b38acae1ad7d017785e:1">`clear`</span><span data-offset-key="21b064b731804b38acae1ad7d017785e:2">(</span><span data-offset-key="21b064b731804b38acae1ad7d017785e:3">*domain=None*</span><span data-offset-key="21b064b731804b38acae1ad7d017785e:4">, </span><span data-offset-key="21b064b731804b38acae1ad7d017785e:5">*path=None*</span><span data-offset-key="21b064b731804b38acae1ad7d017785e:6">, </span><span data-offset-key="21b064b731804b38acae1ad7d017785e:7">*name=None*</span><span data-offset-key="21b064b731804b38acae1ad7d017785e:8">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="421bbb3dbc6d4fa796ca1362c5da67eb"><span data-offset-key="421bbb3dbc6d4fa796ca1362c5da67eb:0">Clear some cookies.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ee72e53b789b47a69140368bd7831310"><span data-offset-key="ee72e53b789b47a69140368bd7831310:0">Invoking this method without arguments will clear all cookies. If given a single argument, only cookies belonging to that domain will be removed. If given two arguments, cookies belonging to the specified path within that domain are removed. If given three arguments, then the cookie with the specified name, path and domain is removed.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1b9222a1458d46b99c2dbc9bd93f24d9"><span data-offset-key="1b9222a1458d46b99c2dbc9bd93f24d9:0">Raises KeyError if no matching cookie exists.</span><span data-offset-key="1b9222a1458d46b99c2dbc9bd93f24d9:1">`clear_expired_cookies`</span><span data-offset-key="1b9222a1458d46b99c2dbc9bd93f24d9:2">()</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2215447bd0204e3d8a8d548efffbf91b"><span data-offset-key="2215447bd0204e3d8a8d548efffbf91b:0">Discard all expired cookies.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="9c5b1254e9cd426abfcb3e3a28a9bc20"><span data-offset-key="9c5b1254e9cd426abfcb3e3a28a9bc20:0">You probably don’t need to call this method: expired cookies are never sent back to the server (provided you’re using DefaultCookiePolicy), this method is called by CookieJar itself every so often, and the .save() method won’t save expired cookies anyway (unless you ask otherwise by passing a true ignore\_expires argument).</span><span data-offset-key="9c5b1254e9cd426abfcb3e3a28a9bc20:1">`clear_session_cookies`</span><span data-offset-key="9c5b1254e9cd426abfcb3e3a28a9bc20:2">()</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="55c827b1a84b4ee7adc006329e3d9d47"><span data-offset-key="55c827b1a84b4ee7adc006329e3d9d47:0">The </span><span data-offset-key="55c827b1a84b4ee7adc006329e3d9d47:1">`codes`</span><span data-offset-key="55c827b1a84b4ee7adc006329e3d9d47:2"> object defines a mapping from common names for HTTP statuses to their numerical codes, accessible either as attributes or as dictionary items.</span></span></span>
